 is bhagidaari ke sammaan main apni patni ke naam par sikaa jari kiya

 In this crossroads, where on the one hand there was a tradition of grief and sati of the death of the husband, on the other hand, the responsibility of the mother who was responsible for the upbringing and education of a little prince until he was able to handle the regalia

 iskaa nateeja yah niklaa ki mardwaadi maansikta ne didda ko dian tak qaraar diya
 It was difficult for the male society to understand how a girl with disabilities without elusive powers could rule the entire Kashmir and a large part of the earth for more than four decades? Didda's story is the story of such a heroine's life journey Who started guerrilla techniques to start a kingdom, become the wife of the king of Kashmir and then widow, taking up many wars and winning wars
 Passing through the passage to the that goes from interesting twist, where possibly described developments to become the world's first commando force, unilateral military
 yah kahani saahas, sanyam, kartavya or rashtrabhakti kii gaatha to kahati hi he, maanav man ke vikaar or dwesh kii gaatha bhi sunaati he

 iske baavjood usne janata se judaav jari rakhaa, mandiron kaa nirmaan karaayaa, saare asia ke saath vyapaar or iran tak faile akhand bharat kii simaaon kii raksha ke liye ranneeti nirmaan karaayaa
 All the references of this book take you to that period of history, which is not talked about very often

 One of these 78 Indians, Pankaj Mishra, told over the phone that they were stranded in the city of Tabuk, near the border of Jordan, 1,000 km from Jeddah
 in logon main se adhikansh uttar pradesh or bihar ke nivasee hai
 These people were hired by Mutafil Maintenance and Trading Company, a Tabuk-based company in 2010 through an Indian employer
 mishra ne bataaya ki company ne is varsh kii shuruyaat se unhen vetan dena band kar diya or unke thaharne vaali jagah par koi bhi suvidha nahin di ja rahi he
 Mishra said, we have not been given compulsory medical card and Akana (identity card), and without this we cannot even get out
 niyokta ne yahaan pahunchane ke baad hi hamaare passport le liye the or ab ham is company kii kaid main hai
 Mishra said that they want to return to their country, but cannot come without passport
 in logon ne chah maheene pehle is silsile main jedda sthit bhartiya vanijyik duutavas se bhi sampark kiya tha

 Poisonous substances such as carbon monoxide and tar are found in tobacco and all these substances are fatal for health
 dhumrapaan or dhuen rahit (tambaakoo chabana) donon hi samaan rup se jaanaleva hai
